<tr><td><h3><a href="https://github.com/ej2940/djy/blob/master/gb/20/4/10/n12021364.md#1" target="_blank">神力神迹与神技的磁气民族</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/ej2940/djy/blob/master/gb/20/4/10/n12021364.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2020/04/GettyImages-1198879006-2-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>

作者：何太铭教授
内风水、外风水的“救助”
